ru bzhi'i chos mdzad thams cad dgongs pa bstanH cho 'phral zla ba spre'u'i zla ba laH. rgyud dang bstun nas nyin mo sngags la 'badH. gtor ma mdos dang mnan sreg yang yang byaH. b+h+yo bzlag zor rnams bshams nas chos khrims bca'H. nyan bshad sgom sgrub byed ba'i bstan pa tshugsH. ri rgya klungs rgya lam rgya la sogs 'dzugsH. skye 'gro sems can thams cad bde la bkodH. ces dang /
bsam yas khra 'brug lha sa 'on ljang rdoH. rgyal blon bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang rnams gsoH. them dgu'i 'og tu rgya 'dre thams cad mnanH. tsa ri mkhar ri stag tshang gter sgrom bzhirH. sgrub gnas tshogs 'khor sbyin sreg brgya rtsa byaH. mkho mthing skyer chu pra dun bu chu bzhirH. sman bla tshar brgya sgrol ma'i mchad pa byaH. bum thang byams pa lha khang bstan pa'i sogH. lha sa bsam yas mdo sngags srog yin pasH. so nams 'bad nas mdo sngags bstan pa tshugsH. zhes ru bzhi'i yul khams su 'tshe byed bzlog thabs de ltar byung ba dang / /

smon lam lhan cig btab pa'i mthu btsan pasH. bod yul gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir 'dzom par 'gyurH. khyad par g.yu ru gra zhes bya ba'i phurH. da lta'i lo tsA bai ro tsa na yiH. sku yi sprul ba @# / /
las ldan snying gi buH. bongs snyoms gnas lngar rigs lnga'i rtags rgyas sprasH. gsang ba'i ming ni 'gyur med rdo rje rtsalH. gsang sngags snod ldan nga yi chos la mosH. bco brgyad lo la sbas pa'i gter sgo 'byedH. ces lung gis zin pa'i sprul sku gtar bdag gling pas zab gter bzhes par phyi nang gsang rtags rnams rim par ma 'phyugs pa gal che ba /
'di spyod skyes bur 'du byed rig ma niH. lha lcam sa le'i sprul ba rigs ldan paH. las kyi 'brel bas sprul ba gsum du 'byungH. rat+na mkha' 'gro'i rtags kyis spras pa niH. rta yi lo ba shar gyi phyogs nas 'byungH. mtshan ldan rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rtags 'chang maH. 'brug gi lo ba nub kyi phyogs nas 'byungH. rigs ldan padma mkha' 'gro'i rtags 'chang baH. bya sprel lo ba byang gi phyogs nas 'byungH. 'di gsum sprul sku'i rig mar 'brel ba naH. nyams rtogs gong 'phel tshe yi bar chad selH. 'gro don bstan pa mtha' ru 'phel bar 'gyurH. gsang ba'i mkha' 'gro padma'i rigs 'chang masH. te sgrom gter la dbang zhing spyod par 'gyurH. rigs ldan phyag rgya lnga yi 'du 'khrugs selH. zhes dang /
o dkar brag gi zab gter kha byang lasH. gzhan lang las ldan bsten bya dangH. log spyod spang bya'i skyon tshang baH. gang yin sgib med lung byang bzhinH. mthong nas spang blang gces par bzungH. 'chal bar spyad na rang srog gnodH. mi mthun rkyen dang duH. kha bskyadH. de phyir rtog pa rab tu chugH. don dang lhun no snying gi buH. zhes sogs lung gis zin pa'i gsang yum 'khrul med cig byung tshe spyi sger thams cad kyi legs rgyur mchis gshis rten 'brel 'grig pa gal che'ang /

lo rgyus su /
bdag dang khri srong lde btsan gyisH. sems bskyed smon lam 'phro 'thud nasH. bod kyi rje 'bangs bde skyid darH. de dus blon po nag po yiH. sri langs snyan phra log pa'i tshigH. bar chad gyed pa mang 'byung gisH. chos khrims tshugs pas skyid par 'gyurH. mnga' thang mtha' nas rgyas par 'gyurH. rgyal po'i mnga' thang rgyas pa yisH. smon lam stobs kyis bod 'bangs skyidH. rgyal khams bde zhing skyid par 'gyurH. zhes pa' dus la babs pa'i gnad kyis sde pa gzhin dang mi 'dra ba sogs rtse dga' gzhung rgyug /

nyer brgyad la mchog sprul blo bzang ye shes chibs bsgyur gdong gi mjal khar gser gyi maN+Dal steng gser srang gang gi tshom bu dang bcas bskal brgyar 'tsho dgos pa'i bka' mchis phebs par de 'dun byed cing sku na gzhon skabs thugs gnyer la brtson dgos pa sogs lugs gnyis kyi khyab cha gang che dgos pa'i snyan sgron dang bka' bsga srung mdung phul nas dal 'gros kyis gtsang stod bla ma'i gdan sar gshegs /

dges pa smos pa ltar ma chad cam 'byung res rnam dpyod mchog tu yangs pas gzhung lugs mang por thos pas gtan la phab pa sngags rams pa dag dbang dpal bzang gis 'dzam gling rgyan gyur dpal ldan 'bras spung dang /

rgyal ba'i sras mchog 'gro 'dul rig pa 'dzinH. rgya bod kun tu rtsod bral sprul skur gragsH. rdo rje 'chang dang yon tan dgongs pa mnyamH. bdag 'dra mtsho skyas padma'i 'byung gnas kyisH. rgyal ba 'das nas lo yang zhe gsum naH. spre'u'i lo la ko sha'i gling du 'khrungsH. sum stod nye par rgya gar ayon sogsH. bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan rtsod med seng ger gragsH. bod kyi mnga' thang dgung la reg pa'i dusH. rat+na'i thugs sgrub yang snying 'dus pa'i bskul byang las /

'di ltar nga yi tshes bcu laH. brtson zhing gsol ba 'debs pa'i buH. dus der bdag dang las ldan rje 'bangs rnamsH. smon lam lhan cig btab pa'i mthu btsan pasH. bod 'bangs gangs ri'i khrod du 'dzom par 'gyurH. khyad par g.yu ru gra zhes bya ba'i phurH. da lta'i lo tsA bai ro tsa na yiH. sku yi sprul pa las ldan snying ga buH. zhes pa nas chos bdag lnga'i nang tshan dang /
lung bstan rab gsal me long las /
de tshe skyong byed mtsho yi ming 'dzin dangH. thugs rje'i zer ldan shar phyogs zab gter bdagH. bar chad ma song rten 'brel 'grig pa naH. bod yul 'gro rnams sprin dbar nyi bzhin bdeH. zhes pa dang blon po thang yig tu 'phrin las sprul bzur cam bstan pa yin no sogs mang po'i rgyu mtshan byung yang bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel ba'i lhag bsam yod par bsnyad 'dra zhing /

de nyid las /
pur rgyal sa khi me long dbusH. las can 'di yi rten 'brel mthusH. sprin mthong nyi bzhin re zhig badH. khyad par gdug pa spre'u'i lorH. bar chad bdud kyi g.yo thabs kyisH. phyi ba shol le lor ma song barH. zab mo'i gter 'di thon ba naH. mtha' dmag dus kyi 'khugs bzhiH. rgyal blon chab srid mnga' thang rgyasH. 'phung byed 'god po'i gnya' gnon byedH. bde skyid dpal dang bkra shis shingH. bod kyi 'gra ba bsod nams cheH. a la la sta skal ba bzangH. zhes rten 'brel bsgrig pa'i gnad kyis 'di nyin dga' ldan bstan 'dzin bo shog thu khang gis mgo dkar gyi yul gru rnams rang zhabs su bsdus te yer khen gyis gtsos grong khyer phyed nyis stong /
